 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item 8.01. Other Events </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On December 15, 2004, the principal and interest collected during the preceding calendar month, net of certain adjustments as provided for in the Sale and Servicing
Agreement, dated as of May 1, 2002 (the &#147;Agreement&#148;), between American Honda Receivables Corp., as Seller, American Honda Finance Corporation, as Servicer, Honda Auto Receivables 2002-2 Owner Trust, a Delaware business trust, as Issuer,
Deutsche Bank Trust Company Delaware, as Owner Trustee (the &#147;Owner Trustee&#148;), Citibank, N.A., as Indenture Trustee (the &#147;Indenture Trustee&#148;) were distributed to holders (&#147;Noteholders&#148;) of notes representing undivided
fractional interests in Honda Auto Receivables 2002-2 Owner Trust. In accordance with the Agreement, the Servicer&#146;s Certificate, as defined in the Agreement, was furnished to the Indenture Trustee for the benefit of the Noteholders and, as
such, was distributed by the Indenture Trustee to the Noteholders. A copy of the Servicer&#146;s Certificate is being filed as Exhibit 20 to this Current Report on Form 8-K. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item 9.01 (c). Exhibit 20 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
